<script type="pmdelayedscript" data-cfasync="false" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" data-no-minify="1" data-rocketlazyloadscript="1">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
        mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
            if (mutation.type === 'childList' && mutation.addedNodes.length) {
                mutation.addedNodes.forEach(processNode);
            }
            if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'src') {
                processNode(mutation.target);
            }
        });
    });

    function processNode(node) {
        // Process single node
        if (node.nodeType === 1 && node.tagName === "IMG" && node.src.includes("amazon.com")) {
            node.setAttribute("data-pin-nopin", "true");
        }
        // Process child nodes
        if (node.nodeType === 1 && node.getElementsByTagName) {
            var imgs = node.getElementsByTagName('img');
            for (var i = 0; i < imgs.length; i++) {
                if (imgs[i].src.includes("amazon.com")) {
                    imgs[i].setAttribute("data-pin-nopin", "true");
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Observer configuration
    observer.observe(document.body, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true,
        attributes: true,
        attributeFilter: ['src']
    });

    // Also apply the attribute to images that are already in the DOM
    document.querySelectorAll('img[src*="amazon.com"]').forEach(processNode);
});
</script>
<script type="pmdelayedscript" data-cfasync="false" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" data-no-minify="1" data-rocketlazyloadscript="1">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    // Function to process nodes and remove Pinterest Save buttons
    function processNode(node) {
        if (node.nodeType === 1 && node.matches('.outermost-social-sharing-link-pinterest a.PIN_1718982390102_button_pin.PIN_1718982390102_save')) {
            node.remove();
        }
        if (node.nodeType === 1 && node.getElementsByClassName) {
            var buttons = node.getElementsByClassName('PIN_1718982390102_button_pin');
            for (var i = 0; i < buttons.length; i++) {
                if (buttons[i].classList.contains('PIN_1718982390102_save')) {
                    buttons[i].remove();
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Observer to monitor changes in the DOM
    var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
        mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
            if (mutation.type === 'childList' && mutation.addedNodes.length) {
                mutation.addedNodes.forEach(processNode);
            }
            if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'class') {
                processNode(mutation.target);
            }
        });
    });

    // Observer configuration
    observer.observe(document.body, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true,
        attributes: true,
        attributeFilter: ['class']
    });

    // Also apply the function to elements that are already in the DOM
    document.querySelectorAll('.outermost-social-sharing-link-pinterest a.PIN_1718982390102_button_pin.PIN_1718982390102_save').forEach(processNode);
});
</script>
